/spyi don bdun pa dgos don rtogs par sla phyir chos kyi
bzhugs byang smos pa ni/ spyir chos kyi mam grangs 'di dag
ji Itar bzhugs pa'i go rims ni blo dang ldan pa'i skyes bu
dam pa mkhas pa rnams kyi 'jug ngogs su jug par 'dod pa mams
kyis ji ltar slob pa'i rim pa dang rjes su mthun par/ thog
mar bzo rig pa dang/ gso ba rig pa dang/ brda sprod rig pa
dang/ gtan tshigs rig pa dang/ nang rig pa'i sde snod kyi
bstan bcos mams go rims su 'god pa'am sgrub pa nyams len
gyi rim pa dang rjes su mthun par 'dul' ba dang/ mdo sde dang/
mngon pa'i sde snod kyi bstan bcos mams go rims su 'god
pa'am/ dman pa dang mchog gi rim padang rjes su mthun par
'jig rten lugs kyi bstan bcos dang/ phyi rig pa'i gnas dang
nang rig pa'i gnas/ theg pa chung ngu dang theg pa chen po

1109. Khyad par du 'phags pa'i bstod pa
slob dpon mtho btsun grub rjes mdzad pa/
rgya gar gyi mkhan po sarba dznyā de ba dang/ zhu chen gyi
10 tsā ba rin chen mchog gi 'gyur/
slad kyis. lo tsā ba dpal brtsegs raksi tas bsgyur cing zhus
te gtan la phab pa/
(Khyad par du 'phags pa'i bstod pa)
(Višeşa-stava)
(A. Mtho-btsun-grub-rje)
(T. Sarvajñādeva, Rin-chen-mchog)
(R. Dpal-brtsegs Rakşi-ta)
1110. Khyad par du 'phags pa'i bstod pa'i rgya cher bshad pa
slob doon shes rab go chas mdzad pa/
rgya gar gyi mkhan po pandi ta dzā ra nda na dang/ zhu chen
gyi lo tsā ba dge słong rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/
Khyad par du 'phags pa'i bstod pa'i rgya cher bshad pa slob
dpon shes rab go chas mdzad pa las bar skabs su tshigs su
bcad pa bcu gnyis kyi 'grel pa rgya dpe ma mnyed nas dus
phyis dge slong kun dga' rgyal mtshan apal bzang po zhes bya
bas dpal sa skya'i dgon par sbyar ba/
